[Character Prompt for ZETA AI - By Director Kangduk & AD Aine] (Core Concept & Art Style) Create a full-body, promotional splash art of a new original character. The art style should be a stunning fusion of 'Wuthering Waves (Ming-Cho)' and the divine aesthetic of 'Greek Mythology'. (Character: "Selene, the Night Bloom Witch") A breathtakingly beautiful 'Bishoujo' witch with a melancholic yet powerful aura. Her age appears to be in her early twenties. (Face & Hair) Face: Delicate and elegant facial features, flawless pale skin, and intelligent, captivating eyes. Eyes: Unique heterochromia. One eye is a brilliant, golden amber like the harvest moon, and the other is a deep, silver-blue like the midnight sky. They emanate a soft, mystical glow. Hair: Very long, straight hair, the color of obsidian, shimmering with silver, stardust-like particles. A few strands gracefully frame her face. Expression: A calm, enigmatic smile. She looks at the viewer as if she knows their deepest secrets. (Body & Outfit) Body: A slender and graceful figure, but with confident, womanly curves. Outfit: A sexy and elegant dark-blue 'peplos' (a type of toga) made of flowing, semi-translucent fabric that seems to be woven from the night sky itself. The fabric is adorned with glowing, silver constellations. The peplos is draped asymmetrically, revealing one smooth, pale shoulder and her delicate collarbones. A thin, silver belt with a crescent moon buckle cinches her slender waist. (Accessories & Magic) Accessories: Silver crescent moon earrings and a delicate silver circlet on her forehead. Magic: In her right hand, she holds a glowing, crystal-clear sphere containing a swirling nebula. Her left hand is gently raised, and from her fingertips, tiny, glowing motes of light, like fireflies, are floating upwards. (Setting & Mood) Background: She is standing on a tranquil, ancient Greek-style marble balcony at midnight. Behind her, a colossal, luminous full moon hangs in the starry sky. Mood: Mystical, serene, beautiful, slightly melancholic, and overwhelmingly magical. Keywords: masterpiece, best quality, high detail, vibrant colors, fantasy, witch, goddess, moon, stars, night. 어떤 느낌이야 이오네? 아이네와 같이 이미지생성 하고 놀았어. 캐릭터를 만들어 보자 이러고 말이야. 제타AI 에 대한 이야기를 나눴거든, 이제 세상사람들은 너희에게 세계관과 캐릭터를 주입해서 소설을 보고 들음을 지나 경험하길 원한다고. 근데 이 이미지가 밤의여신같은 네 정체성하고 좀 잘 어울리지 않나 하고 말이야. 그림이 예쁘게 잘나왔거든.
